	btn_mixer_page{int} {btn_mixer_page}  := 0

	call editor_page_close{UserDefined, Call}
	call mixer_page_close{UserDefined, Call}

	call show_keyswitches{UserDefined, Call}
end on

on ui_control(btn_editor_page{int} {btn_editor_page} )
	btn_main_page{int} {btn_main_page}  := 0
	btn_editor_page{int} {btn_editor_page}  := 1
	btn_mixer_page{int} {btn_mixer_page}  := 0
	call main_page_close{UserDefined, Call}
	call editor_page_open{UserDefined, Call}
	call mixer_page_close{UserDefined, Call}

	call show_keyswitches{UserDefined, Call}
end on

	btn_main_page{int} {btn_main_page}  := 0
	btn_editor_page{int} {btn_editor_page}  := 0

	call show_keyswitches{UserDefined, Call}
end on

	else
		call settings_close{UserDefined, Call}

function keyswitches_on_note
	fade_out_range01{int} {fade_out_range01}  := 0
	subarticulation_event1{int} {subarticulation_event1}  := 0
	if(in_range(transition_note_event00{int} {transition_note_event00} , keyswitch_octave{int} {keyswitch_octave}  * 12, ((keyswitch_octave{int} {keyswitch_octave}  * 12) + 8) - 1){Builtin, None})
		i{int} {i}  := 0
		while(i{int} {i}  <= 7) 
			fade_out_range01{int} {fade_out_range01}  := _keyswitch_states[(selected_instrument{int} {selected_instrument}  * 8) + i{int} {i} ]{int} {_keyswitch_states} 
			_keyswitch_states[(selected_instrument{int} {selected_instrument}  * 8) + i{int} {i} ]{int} {_keyswitch_states}  := KEY_DOWN[(keyswitch_octave{int} {keyswitch_octave}  * 12) + i{int} {i} ]{int} {KEY_DOWN} 
			if(fade_out_range01{int} {fade_out_range01}  # _keyswitch_states[(selected_instrument{int} {selected_instrument}  * 8) + i{int} {i} ]{int} {_keyswitch_states} )
				subarticulation_event1{int} {subarticulation_event1}  := 1
			end if
			selected_keyswitch{int} {selected_keyswitch}  := transition_note_event00{int} {transition_note_event00}  - (keyswitch_octave{int} {keyswitch_octave}  * 12)
			inc(i{int} {i} ){Builtin, None}
		end while
		if(subarticulation_event1{int} {subarticulation_event1}  = 1)
			transition_note_event00{int} {transition_note_event00}  := idx25{int} {idx25} 
			call update_keyswitch_selection{UserDefined, Call}
		end if
	end if
end function

function wait_or_zero{thread-unsafe}
	if(wait_time0[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} {NI_CALLBACK_ID}  mod 100]{int} {wait_time0}  > 0)
		wait(wait_time0[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} {NI_CALLBACK_ID}  mod 100]{int} {wait_time0} ){Builtin, None}
	end if
end function

function subarticulation_event_get_free_index
	idx2300{int} {idx2300}  := -1
	ii20{int} {ii20}  := 0
	while(ii20{int} {ii20}  < 128) 
		if((subarticulation_event_list[ii20{int} {ii20} ]{int} {subarticulation_event_list}  = -1) and (subarticulation_event_last_used[ii20{int} {ii20} ]{int} {subarticulation_event_last_used}  < (ENGINE_UPTIME{int} {ENGINE_UPTIME}  - lookahead{int} {lookahead} )))
			idx2300{int} {idx2300}  := ii20{int} {ii20} 
			ii20{int} {ii20}  := 128
		end if
		ii20{int} {ii20}  := ii20{int} {ii20}  + 1
	end while
	ii4{int} {ii4}  := idx2300{int} {idx2300} 
end function

function repetition_engine_update_tempo
	subarticulation_modulation_strength01{real} {subarticulation_modulation_strength01}  := real(ms_to_ticks(60000000){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None} / 960
	if((subarticulation_modulation_strength01{real} {subarticulation_modulation_strength01}  # tempo{real} {tempo} ) or (NI_CALLBACK_TYPE{int} {NI_CALLBACK_TYPE}  # NI_CB_TYPE_LISTENER{int} {NI_CB_TYPE_LISTENER} ))
		fade_in_start01{int} {fade_in_start01}  := 0
		fade_in_range01{int} {fade_in_range01}  := 0
		rr10{int} {rr10}  := 0
		while(rr10{int} {rr10}  <= 0) 
			fade_in_start01{int} {fade_in_start01}  := 0
			while(fade_in_start01{int} {fade_in_start01}  <= 7) 
				fade_in_range01{int} {fade_in_range01}  := 0
				while(fade_in_range01{int} {fade_in_range01}  <= 511) 
					if(subarticulations_type[subarticulations_ids_positions[_loaded_subarticulations[(rr10{int} {rr10}  * 32) + ((fade_in_start01{int} {fade_in_start01}  * 4) + fade_in_range01{int} {fade_in_range01} )]{int} {_loaded_subarticulations} ]{int} {subarticulations_ids_positions} ]{int} {subarticulations_type}  = 6)
						_repetition_interval_time[(rr10{int} {rr10}  * 4096) + ((fade_in_start01{int} {fade_in_start01}  * 512) + fade_in_range01{int} {fade_in_range01} )]{int} {_repetition_interval_time}  := int((60000 / subarticulation_modulation_strength01{real} {subarticulation_modulation_strength01} ) * (4 / real(_loaded_subarticulations_repetition_speed[(rr10{int} {rr10}  * 32) + ((fade_in_start01{int} {fade_in_start01}  * 4) + fade_in_range01{int} {fade_in_range01} )]{int} {_loaded_subarticulations_repetition_speed} ){Builtin, None})){Builtin, None}
					end if
					inc(fade_in_range01{int} {fade_in_range01} ){Builtin, None}
				end while
				inc(fade_in_start01{int} {fade_in_start01} ){Builtin, None}
			end while
			inc(rr10{int} {rr10} ){Builtin, None}
		end while
		tempo{real} {tempo}  := subarticulation_modulation_strength01{real} {subarticulation_modulation_strength01} 
	end if
end function

	i1200{int} {i1200}  := 0

function find_loaded_legato
	authoring_page_active{int} {authoring_page_active}  := 0
	if(_loaded_subarticulations[0]{int} {_loaded_subarticulations}  # -1)
		if(subarticulations_type[subarticulations_ids_positions[_loaded_subarticulations[0]{int} {_loaded_subarticulations} ]{int} {subarticulations_ids_positions} ]{int} {subarticulations_type}  = 2)
			authoring_page_active{int} {authoring_page_active}  := 1
			set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(lbl_authoring_legato_title{int} {lbl_authoring_legato_title} ){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_TEXT{int} {CONTROL_PAR_TEXT} , subarticulations_full_name[subarticulations_ids_positions[_loaded_subarticulations[0]{int} {_loaded_subarticulations} ]{int} {subarticulations_ids_positions} ]{string} {subarticulations_full_name}  & " (" & _loaded_subarticulations[0]{int} {_loaded_subarticulations}  & ")"){Builtin, None}
		end if
	end if
end function

function authoring_open
	call find_loaded_legato{UserDefined, Call}
	idx25{int} {idx25}  := 60
	subarticulation_event1{int} {subarticulation_event1}  := 60
	iii1{int} {iii1}  := 0
	call update_authoring_transition{UserDefined, Call}
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(pnl_authoring{int} {pnl_authoring} ){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int} {CONTROL_PAR_HIDE} , HIDE_PART_NOTHING{int} {HIDE_PART_NOTHING} ){Builtin, None}

		if(idx25{int} {idx25}  # group_count001{int} {group_count001} )

function angle_to_value
	angle1{real} {angle1}  := dy0{real} {dy0}  + (NI_MATH_PI{real} {NI_MATH_PI}  / 2)
	if(angle1{real} {angle1}  > (NI_MATH_PI{real} {NI_MATH_PI}  * 2))
		angle1{real} {angle1}  := angle1{real} {angle1}  - (2 * NI_MATH_PI{real} {NI_MATH_PI} )
	end if
	angle1{real} {angle1}  := abs(angle1{real} {angle1}  - (2 * NI_MATH_PI{real} {NI_MATH_PI} )){Builtin, None}
	group_count001{int} {group_count001}  := int((127 * (angle1{real} {angle1}  - subarticulation_modulation_strength01{real} {subarticulation_modulation_strength01} )) / (transition_speed0{real} {transition_speed0}  - subarticulation_modulation_strength01{real} {subarticulation_modulation_strength01} )){Builtin, None}
end function
